Mussolini Warns the League of Nations, Resolves to Send Representatives to Attend on September 4th, To Express Italy's Position to the World 33

(London) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, in an interview with Daily Mail special correspondent Price, said: "Regarding the Abyssinian issue, Italy will not back down. If the Italian government changes its attitude, the 200,000 Italian troops currently stationed in East Africa will act on their own, and the government will not be able to stop them. If the League of Nations decides to impose sanctions on Italy, Italy will immediately withdraw from the League of Nations. Know that no matter who wants to impose sanctions on Italy, the entire Italian people are ready to use force to oppose them. If the League of Nations handles the matter carelessly and wants to turn Italy's colonial war into a European conflict, causing all ambitious countries in Europe and the world to be greedy and have designs on others, then the cost will be more than the lives of millions of people, and tens of millions of people will be reduced to insects and sand. Then the responsibility for this should be borne solely by the League of Nations. When the Council of the League of Nations meets on September 4th, I will send a delegation to attend, with the intention of clearly expressing Italy's position to the world. I will use documents and photos as supporting evidence for Italy's claims, and I will send a box of books to Geneva to reveal the customs of the savage Abyssinian people and the prevailing slave system in that country. After the League of Nations has carefully examined these documents, we will wait and see whether our country will still be treated the same as Abyssinia." Mussolini also said that Italy is willing to cooperate with all countries, as evidenced by the signing of the Locarno Treaty in 1924 and the formation of the Anglo-French-Italian joint front at the Stresa Conference this year. Italy assisted the British Empire during the war and when the whole world united against it. This must be solemnly declared. Price then asked Mussolini if there was any possibility of Italy changing its attitude. Mussolini replied no. Price asked again whether the Rome Agreement concluded between Italy and France on January 7th, which resolved the outstanding issues between the two countries, included a clause stating that France allowed Italy to have favorable treatment in East Africa. Is this true? The Italian Prime Minister replied, "The Rome Agreement resolved all the disputes between our country and France. That is true." In addition, the Italian Prime Minister believes that the time has come to discuss the entire colonial issue, saying that if Abyssinia can be opened up for colonial business, Italy's wishes can be satisfied. (Havas Telegram, 26th)

Italian Cabinet Holds Special Meeting, Today in Bolzano 34

(Rome) The Italian cabinet is scheduled to hold a special meeting in Bolzano tomorrow. Mussolini arrived there this afternoon to participate in the army's grand maneuvers. The Secretary-General of the Fascist Party is accompanying him. This exercise centers on Bolzano because the city is located in a mountainous area. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

(Rome) While Mussolini conducts a large-scale exercise with 500,000 troops in northern Italy to respond to the hopes of European peace negotiators, he issued another order today to send 7,000 troops from the port of Naples to East Africa. According to estimates here, Italy's military expenditure on Africa amounts to 5 million to 10 million lire per day. (National Society Telegram, 26th)

(Rome) Recently, Italian public opinion no longer feels interested in the diplomatic progress of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. News such as the failure of the Paris Tripartite Conference, the passage of the Neutrality Act by the U.S. Congress, and the situation of the British cabinet meeting have all been received here with indifference. All attention is focused on rapidly completing military preparations. Regarding aviation facilities, the air traffic between Italy and East Africa is becoming more convenient. In January of this year, there were only thirteen airfields in the Italian territory of Eritrea. Now, the number has increased to fifteen. The Asmara-to-Keren air route has two round trips per week. Each flight carries 150 kilograms of mail and five passengers. It takes only three days to reach Asmara from Rome, which is quite convenient. Furthermore, the number of people enlisting in the army in Italy has not decreased. All members of the Turin Fascist Party branch and the leaders of other branches have been incorporated into the army. Veterans in places such as Pola, Trieste, and Genoa are also eager to join the army, which shows the enthusiasm of the people. According to reports, the Kingdom of Yemen in the Arabian Peninsula has decided to remain neutral in the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. This news has had a profound impact on public opinion. The Abyssinian government sent representatives to Yemen two years ago to establish friendly relations in order to strengthen the friendship between the two countries. Yemen's current decision to remain neutral shows that Abyssinia's plans have not been effective. (Havas, 26th)

The Italian Embassy here has ordered Italian citizens to leave Abyssinia as soon as possible. Although the British and French embassies have not issued similar orders to British and French citizens, the British Embassy has told British citizens and Northern European missionaries under British protection residing in various provinces of Abyssinia that it is best to move to Addis Ababa early for protection. The War Office recently explained the reason for this move, saying that strengthening the forces in Malta and Aden had already been decided last year. This is just a rehash of the old plan. Moreover, about one hundred of the soldiers sent are carrying their families. If there is a danger in the above-mentioned two places, it would be impossible for the soldiers to bring their families. Malta currently has a garrison of 33,000 troops, and Aden has a force of only about 250 troops. Therefore, the transfer of ships is not surprising. (Havas Telegram, 26th)

(Tokyo) A national meeting of army commanders and division commanders, aimed at controlling the military and rectifying military discipline, was held at 9:00 AM on the 26th in the First Conference Room of the Army Ministry. Army Minister Hayashi delivered a speech on the important principles of military purification, advocating for the rectification of military discipline throughout the army and the control of the army. The meeting concluded at noon, followed by a luncheon and adjourned at 1:00 PM. (Domei News Agency, 26th)

(Tokyo) The Army Ministry announced the military purification policy instructed by Army Minister Hayashi at today's division commander meeting, the contents of which are as follows: The current situation is serious, with many internal and external affairs. It is an increasingly urgent time for national unity and the revitalization of military discipline. Suddenly, an ominous incident, unprecedented in the history of the Imperial Army, occurred within the military, causing unspeakable fear. Considering the glorious history of the Imperial Army, regardless of the cause, it is a matter of deep regret. This is due to my own lack of virtue, and my responsibility is undoubtedly great. I am confident that with the efforts of all commanders, the entire army will not be shaken by this incident. However, in light of the impact of the current situation and the incident, I am determined to quickly complete the purification of military discipline and the strengthening of unity, to advance towards the goal with unified efforts from top to bottom. Therefore, I have convened this meeting. The life of the military is based on the strong unity of a consistently controlled network. All officers of the Imperial Army must thoroughly understand the essence of military construction, clearly recognize the truth of the Emperor's command of the military with the concept of the Emperor personally leading the troops, and ensure that all actions adhere to the consistent system of command. Officers must be cautious in their words and actions, make contact with their subordinates, and ensure the authority of the military. At the same time, it is essential to strictly protect military secrets. Furthermore, it is necessary to discern the truth from falsehood in rumors and gossip and severely crack down on their dissemination. Those who lead subordinates should guide their subordinates with love and enthusiasm, teaching and nurturing them. If there is no sign of repentance, they should be dealt with decisively. Furthermore, subordinates should always respect their superiors, accept their teachings, and not disrupt the order by publicizing their own beliefs. In short, the current situation is serious, and it is essential to thoroughly understand the consciousness of the Imperial Army, to rely on and trust each other from top to bottom, and to complete the practice with the unity of the entire nation, in accordance with the Emperor's will. (Domei News Agency, 26th)

(Tokyo) Because Army Minister Hayashi's instructions were chosen with the best possible words, the internal circles expressed their approval. However, the problem lies in how to fully realize each point of these instructions. The Army Minister did not exhaust his abilities with a single instruction. He has made a significant determination to devise good measures for the future. Therefore, how the Army Minister will handle various important issues from now on and achieve the ideal of military purification is attracting great attention from the general public. (Domei News Agency, 26th)

Army Minister Hayashi feels deeply responsible for the occurrence of the Nagata Incident and is working hard to implement measures to rectify military discipline and control the military. He convened a division commander meeting on the 25th and held a meeting of directors of directly affiliated government agencies and school principals on the 26th, delivering important instructions. However, it will take three to four weeks for these instructions to thoroughly reach the entire army. The Army Minister will clarify his responsibility and decide on his course of action after this matter has come to a conclusion. (Domei News Agency, 26th)

Takahashi Holds Hayama Conference to Review Budget Requests; Difference Between Income and Expenditure is Approximately 1.4 Billion 44

Hayama: The first meeting of the Ministry of Finance to determine the outline of the general accounting budget for the next year was held in Hayama today. During the meeting, Budget Bureau Director-General Kaya stated that the new budget requests from various ministries had reached 859 million yuan. If the 300 million yuan reserved by the various ministries is added, the total reaches 1.159 billion yuan. After calculation and consolidation, the revised standard budget is 1.661 billion yuan. Combined with the aforementioned new requests, the total budget for the next year actually reaches a huge sum of 2.82 billion yuan. On the revenue side, even with the inclusion of natural revenue increases, ordinary revenue will only be in the range of 1.4 billion to 1.5 billion yuan. Comparing income and expenditure, the shortfall will inevitably be the same as last year, and it will be necessary to issue public bonds. Therefore, the fiscal authorities, while adhering to the principle of gradually reducing deficit bonds, are actually in a position where they cannot avoid strictly limiting new requests and are hoping for the support of Finance Minister Takahashi. Next, the Director-General of the Tax Bureau and the Director-General of the Finance Bureau reported and explained on the situation of tax revenue, the projected situation of natural revenue increases, and public bond policies. After lunch, the meeting resumed. (Domei News Agency, 26th)

(Tokyo) The overall picture of next year's budget has become largely clear. Meningitis in Tokyo Threatens to Spread Throughout Japan; 99 New Cases in One Day; Doctors Determine Spread by Small Red Mosquitoes 46

(Tokyo) Between the morning of the 25th and the morning of the 26th, the number of meningitis cases in Tokyo suddenly increased by 99, causing extreme panic among the citizens. Since the 1st, the total number of patients has reached 219. In addition, patients have also been appearing in Kanagawa, Shizuoka, Yamanashi, Fukushima, and Nagano prefectures, threatening to spread throughout the country. (Rengo News, 26th)

(Tokyo) The number of sleeping sickness cases in Tokyo is increasing daily. As of noon today, there have been a total of 254 cases, with a sudden increase of 58 cases last night. Most of the patients are children under the age of ten. (Reuters, 26th) According to a report from the Metropolitan Police Department's Disease Prevention Section, there were another 24 new cases of sleeping sickness from noon to 7:00 PM on the 25th, two of whom have already died. To date, the total number of patients since August is 184, of whom 25 have died. (Dentsu News Agency, 26th)

(Tokyo) Since the outbreak of lethargic encephalitis in Japan on the 24th, there have been many patients in various regions. According to an investigation by the Ministry of Home Affairs, the current situation is as follows: Tokyo City 252, Kanagawa Prefecture 43, Osaka City 50, Kyoto Prefecture 52, Yamanashi Prefecture 37, Shizuoka Prefecture 74, Fukushima Prefecture 2, Sendai 1, Gifu Prefecture 6, Yokohama City 4, totaling 521. (China United Press, 26th)

Okayama: Dr. Mitabayashi announced the results of his research on the epidemic state of lethargic encephalitis at Okayama Medical University, saying that although this disease exists in the United States, it is originally a unique epidemic in Japan. According to research to date, it is not directly transmitted between people, but is transmitted to humans by extremely small red mosquitoes. These mosquitoes hide in people's homes day and night. Methods to study the source of the disease and prevent it can be researched during the day. The most important thing is to take care to avoid being bitten by mosquitoes. (Dentsu News Agency, 26th)

Number of Mental Patients in Taiwan: According to Statistics, Over 3,000 Across the Island 47

Taipei: Due to the increasing pressure of life and other unfortunate events, the number of people suffering from mental illness in Taiwan is increasing year by year. Currently, there are a total of six mental hospitals in Taiwan, including Yangshen Yuan, Yanghao Tang, Renji Yuan, Aiai Liao, Aihu Society in Tainan, and Kaohsiung Tzu Hui Society, both public and private. According to the survey statistics at the end of May this year, there are 303 people under confinement, 454 people who have been under confinement, 421 people requiring monitoring, and a total of 3,313 other patients. However, if a more thorough investigation is conducted, the number could be nearly double that. The supervision of mental patients in Taiwan's mental hospitals currently has no legal basis. Only their close relatives can have them admitted. Malignant mental patients cannot be forcibly admitted, which is extremely inconvenient. Therefore, the Governor-General's Health Department has been studying the implementation of the Mental Hospital Law and the Mental Patient Supervision Law, which are currently under vigorous study. This time, the two laws implemented in mainland Japan at the end of March of the eighth year of Taisho will be used as the basis. The draft has already been completed and is currently under review by the Legal Bureau. It will be implemented soon, with the aim of preventing disturbances to order through passive methods. (China United Press, 26th)

Japan Plans to Manipulate North China's Cotton Industry Through Loans, Japanese Consul in Rehe Conducts Dredging of the Luan River 70

Tianjin Correspondence: Earlier this month, Mr. Funatsu Ten'ichirō, the managing director of the Japan Cotton Spinners' Association in China, came to Tianjin from Shanghai to conduct a detailed survey of the cotton spinning industry in North China. He returned to Japan last week. After arriving in Tokyo, Funatsu gave a speech stating that it was not yet the right time for Japanese investment in the North China cotton spinning industry. However, the reality is quite the opposite of what he said. After Funatsu left, he entrusted the Tōtaku K.K., the Daifuku Company, and Itō, the director of the Jin Yu Da Cotton Mill, to provide loans, intending to use loans to acquire the stock rights of various cotton mills as a step towards future manipulation. The so-called North China cotton mills, with the exception of the Tangshan Hua Xin Cotton Mill, are all located in Tianjin. Therefore, it is more accurate to call them the Tianjin cotton industry. Traditionally, there have been six mills in total. Currently, only Hua Xin, (Tianjin Mill) Doucheng, and Yudai are operating. The others, such as Yu Yuan, Beiyang, and Hengyuan, have all suspended operations. Yu Da was originally operated by Chinese, but due to debts owed to the Japanese, it has become a creditor-controlled enterprise, practically equivalent to a Japanese-owned mill. Therefore, of the six cotton mills in Tianjin, only two are still managed by Chinese, with the others either bankrupt or under Japanese management. Due to the dumping of Japanese yarn, business has been difficult for a long time. Although Yu Yuan, Heng Yuan, and Bei Yang intend to resume operations, due to financial constraints, preparations have been ongoing for almost a year without a definite date. Only Hengyuan has a rumor that people will be sent by the creditor Central Bank and other banks to manage the resumption of work, but when this will be realized is also unknown. The Japanese side recognizes this as an opportunity, hence the visit of Funatsu Ten'ichirō to conduct inspections and the activities of Daifuku and Tōtaku. It is faintly heard that considerable success has already been achieved, and soon one or two cotton mills may be resurrected under the guise of Japanese guidance.

Within the past week, Nakane, the Japanese consul stationed in Chengde, Rehe, along with Yamagishi Sadaichi, the chief of the civil engineering section of the puppet Chengde public office, advisor Chiba, and seven attendants, inspected the Luan River downstream to the Tonghe at the river mouth. Afterwards, Yamagishi, Nakane, Chiba, and others came to Tianjin to meet with Kawa Shigeru, the Japanese Consul-General in Tianjin, and members of the garrison military department. On the 23rd, they returned to Chengde to report. The purpose of the inspection was to dredge the Luan River to make it directly accessible to the sea, so as to serve as an outlet for Rehe and a channel for economic communication between southern Rehe and northern Hebei. Traditionally, the products of Rehe Province are transported by land, which is quite inconvenient. Moreover, the need for materials and local products cannot be severed with Hebei Province, so this plan has been formulated, with the expectation of certain success. The results of Yamagishi and others' inspection are quite satisfactory, and their forecast may be implemented soon. (24th)

Suzhou: Opening Ceremony for the Su-Mu Road 72

Yesterday (26th) was the date for the opening ceremony of the Su-Mu Road. The western suburbs of Suzhou have long been known as a scenic area. After the completion of the road, it runs north from Hanshan Temple, then east through the Xituan Liuyuan Road, exiting at the Qing Tang and turning south, passing through the Xikuatang Qizishan to the town of Mudu, at the foot of Lingyan Mountain, turning west directly to Tianpingshan, forming a square loop. Only the section from west of Hanshan Temple to Tianpingshan has not been built. As for branch lines, one line runs from Mudu to Dongting Dongshan, and another line runs directly to Guangfu Dengwei. Hengtang to Shihou Shangfang Mountain are all under design and construction. Zhangyuan to Mi Du Bridge Baodai Bridge also has a road to follow, only the section from Baodai Bridge to Hehua Dang is yet to be built. The Western Garden to Tiger Hill and Liuyuan to the Shanghai-Suzhou Railway Station all have roads accessible. The entire Su-Mu Road is 117.9 kilometers long. Arches have been erected at the starting point of the Gordon Bridge outside Panmen and at the Mudu train station. A large number of guests arrived. At 11:00 AM, County Magistrate Wu Qiyun held the ribbon-cutting ceremony. The Suzhou-Fukong Company's cars carrying guests then drove forward. The journey was smooth. The company also hosted tea and refreshments at the Shi Jia Hotel, followed by a tour of Lingyan Mountain. Many private cars also participated in the tour of Lingyan Mountain. When departing, one car belonging to painter Wu Silan overturned in a field at the No. 1 bridge due to excessive speed, and his wife was slightly injured.

The day before yesterday evening, accompanied by Wu Xuyong and Zhao Xuchang from the Wuxi County Anti-Smoking Association, along with police officers from the fifth precinct of the Public Security Bureau, they rushed to the Dachang Opium Store in Zhuchang Alley to conduct a thorough inspection for four hours. Subsequently, at the home of the landlord Li, they found Lü Yizheng, who was smoking without a license, and Li Yao, who was providing opium for others to smoke. They were both taken to the county. At the same time, Zhou Rongchang, an opium dealer, was found in Hele Lane in Nancangmen, along with ten taels of opium, stamped with the hard-printed Dachang chop. Furthermore, Liu Afu, an opium dealer, was found in Jiulong Lane on the road. Yesterday, all were taken to the county.

Yu Gui, a woman from Sizhangwan outside the South Gate, is the daughter of Yu Binggen, who works in aquatic products at No. 135 there. She married Sheng Shou as an adopted son-in-law in the East Gate. They have been married for many years and have had two children. Recently, Yu Gui became pregnant again. After only seven months, she suddenly went into labor the day before yesterday. A midwife was called to deliver the baby, but for four days the fetus did not descend, which everyone found strange. On the morning of the 24th, she suddenly gave birth to more than ten small snakes, the larger ones about a foot long, and the smaller ones four or five inches long, all wriggling. Yangzhou: Weak Woman Commits Suicide Due to Intolerable Abuse 76

Zhang Cunxi, a farmer from Xiaotang Village in the southern part of the county, has two sons. The elder son farms at home, and the younger son works as a tailor in Shanghai. Two years ago, Cunxi married Xiao Zhengtai's eldest daughter from Jiaolizhuang to his younger son as his wife. Unexpectedly, after the younger daughter-in-law, Xiao, entered the family, she was abused by her brother-in-law, Renbao. The other day, Xiao could not bear the suffering and committed suicide by drowning. Her brother rushed to the scene after hearing the news, but instead of providing assistance, he pressed Xiao into the water, nearly drowning her. After being persuaded by Wang Lin, he went home. She was again beaten and scolded by Renbao. By noon the next day, Cunxi noticed that his daughter-in-law had not left the room. He called, but there was no response. Knowing something had happened, he broke open the door and found that she had hanged herself from the beam.

Special Article

Confucius's Daily Life and Interpretation of Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Sense of Shame 77

— Kong Xiangxi

Since the Han Dynasty, China has revered Confucius. All aspects of national politics, economy, and the people's thoughts and lives have been guided by the teachings of Confucius. For over two thousand years, the continuation of national life and the flourishing of Eastern culture have been inseparable from his teachings. However, since the opening of the country to foreign influences and the influx of Western culture, the Chinese people have suddenly lost confidence. Conflicting views on safety and different perspectives on what to adopt and discard have emerged. Those who are infatuated with modern theories often seek novelty and difference, even advocating for the overthrow of Confucianism. With the foundation shaken, social customs have gradually deteriorated, causing concern among those who are aware of the times. As a descendant of the Sage and having heard the late Premier's call to restore traditional morality to save China, at a time when the nation is in decline and in need of urgent salvation, I originally intended to write about the thoughts and actions of the Sage based on my limited knowledge, focusing on the Analects. Coinciding with the Sage's birthday, I dare to present a table summarizing the Sage's daily life and his teachings on propriety, justice, integrity, and sense of shame. Although times have changed, the Sage's words and actions may not be fully imitable, but if all compatriots can emulate his rigorous and disciplined spirit, the social customs will naturally undergo a transformation. Only then can we jointly strive for the cause of national revival. This is my humble intention. The first part concerns the Sage's daily life, divided into material, spiritual, and conversational aspects. The material aspects, including clothing, food, housing, and travel, are sufficient to establish a new standard of living. The spiritual aspects include the pursuit of struggle, harmony, joy, comfort, love, humility, diligence, respect, and thoroughness. Conversations are divided into elegant speech, rare speech, and silence. The model set forth serves as a template for all. The second part concerns the Sage's discussions on propriety, justice, integrity, and sense of shame. The Analects contains the word "propriety" (禮) but not "unreasonableness" (無理). The Sage aimed to guide the people into a structured way of life and did not wish to engage in empty talk of human nature. Therefore, propriety is about conduct (履), enabling people to act together. I now present its outline, dividing it into categories. Justice (義) means appropriateness (宜), tailoring things to be appropriate. The Analects discusses how to act in various situations, acquire wealth, interact with others, manage affairs, speak, serve the ruler, and govern the people, providing a path of justice to follow, so that the people's morals have a principle. Integrity (廉) means self-restraint (歛), extended to mean upholding integrity and being able to restrain oneself. The Analects contains one instance of the word "integrity" (廉), which originally meant self-restraint, not the virtue of incorruptibility. Only Gong Wei's lack of desire was interpreted by earlier scholars using the word "integrity." The frugality of cultivating integrity, the way to deal with wealth, the effect of advocating integrity, and the distinction between righteousness and profit are all deeply and clearly stated. The character for "shame" (恥) consists of "ear" (耳) and "heart" (心), signifying the feeling of shame upon hearing wrongdoing. When people feel ashamed, their ears turn red and their faces flush, which is the sign of it. The Doctrine of the Mean says that knowing shame is close to courage. Wang Chuanshan said that shame is easy but knowing is difficult, and only by knowing what to choose can one be considered to have shame. Now, observing the Analects' earnest teaching on shame, I list the four major aspects of conduct, interpersonal relations, civilizing the people, and interacting with neighbors to clarify what to choose. I have also included the different schools of thought within the Confucian tradition, with explanations for each, hoping to discuss them with fellow countrymen and gentlemen who admire Confucianism and discuss national affairs.

Note 1: See Bai Hu Tong. Note 2: See Erya Notes.

Note 3: See Shi Ming. Note 4: See Shi Ming.

Note 5: Based on Su Xing's theory, see Wang Xianqian's Shi Ming Shu Zheng Bu Suo Yin.

Note 6: See Liu Shu Zong Yao. Note 7: See Chuanshan's posthumous writings.

Note 1: Liu Baonan's Lun Yu Shuo Zheng Yi quotes Wei Zhao's commentary on Guo Yu: "Yan means extreme." Confucius himself spoke of coarse rice and plain water, finding joy in them. He praised Yan Hui's simple meals and drinking water from a gourd, and Yu's plain food and drink. He also said that scholars should be ashamed of wearing poor clothes and eating poor food, which is not worth discussing. Here, he meant that he did not eat the most refined food or the most finely sliced meat. Liu's statement is correct.

Note 2: Xu Lianxuan's Confucius' Life states: "There is no record of Confucius' residence in the Analects Xiangdang Chapter. Other chapters and many books relating to and discussing Confucius also do not mention it." Confucius was a person who valued consistency between words and actions. Based on what he said, we can infer where he lived.

Note 3: Yu Zhengbian's Gui Yi Cun Gao: "The Book of Poetry and the Book of Documents are extensively quoted, and propriety must be spoken in accordance with the person and the time. Speak of benevolence to the father, and filial piety to the son. Elegant speech is the execution of propriety."

Note: Yang Shouchang of the Education Magazine's Special Issue on Reading the Classics says: "The words 'ruler' and 'minister' are merely pronouns for leader and assistant. Therefore, the names of ruler and minister can be changed, but the reality of ruler and minister remains. The rituals of bowing up and down need not be the same, but the assistant must have a corresponding respect for the leader."

Chen Peng's Dongshu Reading Notes: "The Analects mentions propriety in over forty chapters. From personal listening, speech, and action, to matters related to teaching children, serving the ruler, employing ministers, and governing the people, all are done with propriety. The aspects of propriety include reverence, deference, frugality, moderation, and culture. Its foundation lies in thrift, its application in harmony, and it is preceded by benevolence, righteousness, extensive learning, and different priorities for the advanced and the backward. If the backward follow the advanced, propriety, though abandoned, is still cherished. The Rites of Xia and Yin are insufficient to prove, yet can still be spoken of. The saying that archery is not about piercing the hide describes the text of the Book of Rites. The Xiangdang chapter is similar to the Records of Rites. The Analects' discussion of propriety is extensive and precise, and its exploration is inexhaustible. All that the Analects speaks of is propriety. Looking at the small things, such as walking quickly, is the propriety of the son seeing his father; bathing is the propriety of the minister seeing the ruler; offering a bundle of dried meat is the propriety of the disciple seeing the teacher for the first time; not arriving unless on public business is the propriety of the scholar seeing the official; three evasions is the impropriety of sitting beside; sitting in a position alongside the teacher is the impropriety of the student. The small things are like this, and the large things can be known."

Note: Huang Yizhou's Jing Xun Bi Yi: "The Doctrine of the Mean: 'Justice is appropriateness.' The Record of Sacrifices: 'Justice is this appropriateness.' The Record of Music: 'Justice rectifies it.' The Record of Rites: 'Justice is the standard of the world.' Jia Yi said: 'Conduct that is appropriate is called justice, and the opposite is called ignorance.' Note: Justice means appropriateness, the ability of the heart to judge right and wrong and act accordingly. Rectification and standards mean that justice can judge, this is the correct explanation of justice." Wen Yumin's Lun Yu Research: "To understand the true meaning of justice, one must first understand the boundaries between justice and propriety. Propriety is applied to a fixed name or a fixed event as a norm. However, human affairs are constantly changing, and there are fluid entities that cannot be named, and there are changing events that cannot be named, and there are some trivial events that cannot be named. Such facts cannot be governed by propriety, and it is necessary to advocate a sense of justice as a criterion for such affairs. Therefore, propriety is to maintain constancy, and justice is to adapt to change. This is the distinction between propriety and justice."

Note 1: Wang Fuzhi's Si Jie: "Learning is easy but liking is difficult, action is easy but striving is difficult, shame is easy but knowing is difficult. Not liking learning, not striving to act, all are not knowing shame and being ashamed of what is not worthy of shame. Therefore, shame must know how to choose, and then it can be said to have shame."

Note 2: Yan Yuan's Si Shu Zheng Wu: "In a country with the Way, one cannot serve the ruler and benefit the people, bringing about the governance of Tang and Yu, but only eating leisurely salary. In a country without the Way, one cannot help with difficulties and support danger, protecting the country, but only eating leisurely salary, this is deeply shameful." When there is the Way, being unable to jointly assist in great governance, but hiding away to claim nobility; when there is no Way, being unable to jointly perform the merit of restoring order, but only greedily seeking temporary wealth and honor, then their shame is the same. (To be continued)

Local News

Confucius's Birthday Commemorated Today, All Sectors Hold Commemorative Meetings, Holiday One Day, Flags Raised in Celebration 78

Today is the anniversary of Confucius's birthday. The city party headquarters and the city government have convened representatives from all sectors of the city to hold a commemorative meeting at 10:00 AM in the Dacheng Hall of the Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road. The details are as follows:

Party and Government Announcement

The city party headquarters and the city government issued an announcement to commemorate Confucius's birthday, stating that the 27th of this month is the National Teacher Confucius Memorial Day. All sectors will have a day off and flags will be raised in celebration. It is also decided to convene all sectors at 10:00 AM on that morning to hold a commemorative meeting in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road in the South City. All sectors and groups in the city are notified to send one representative to attend the commemorative meeting on time. This announcement is hereby issued.

Commemoration by All Sectors

Confucius's birthday is a national memorial day. The city party headquarters and the city government have followed the central government's regulations and convened representatives from all organs, groups, factories, and schools to hold a grand commemorative meeting at 10:00 AM today in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road. In addition to sending representatives to attend the commemorative meeting today, all organs, groups, factories, and schools in the city will raise flags and have a day off or suspend work. The local post offices will also reduce the number of shifts according to the weekly holiday system. Banks, money shops, and customs will be closed for one day.

Venue Arrangement

The commemorative meeting venue is located in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road. The party and national flags are hung crosswise on the left and right in front of the gate, and a white bamboo cloth banner is hung in the middle. The party and national flags and bamboo cloth banners are also hung in the same way outside the venue. Memorial slogans and the deeds of Confucius's life are posted around the venue. A portrait of the Premier and the party and national flags are hung on the rostrum, and a portrait of Confucius is placed below. Various ancient musical instruments such as zithers, bells, and drums are displayed on both sides, which is quite solemn.

Meeting Staff

All the members of the conference have also been appointed by the city party headquarters and the city government as follows: Presidium: City Party Headquarters, City Government, Security Department, City Farmers' Association, General Labor Union, City Chamber of Commerce, City Education Association; Reception Director: Li Dachao; Discipline Director: Zhang Yingzeng; Discipline Officers: Yu Yaoqiu, Li Zhixiang, Ren Bin, Yang Dean, Tong Muge, Wu Xianren, Wu Di, Cao Runsen; Recorders: Wang Guoping, Du Mengsen; Master of Ceremonies: Zhang Hanyun.

Commemorative Ceremony

The order of the commemorative meeting has also been arranged as follows: (1) All stand at attention, (2) Play music (Public Security Bureau Military Band), (3) Sing the Party Song, (4) Bow three times to the Party and National Flags and the portrait of the Premier and the portrait of Confucius, (5) The Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will, (6) The Chairman reports the significance of commemorating Confucius, (7) Speech, internal slogans, (9) Play music (Dasihai Orchestra), (10) Ceremony concludes.

Slogans and Banners

(1) Emulate the personality of the sage Confucius, (2) Carry forward the sage Confucius's doctrine, (3) Restore the nation's inherent culture, (4) Promote the nation's inherent spirit, (5) Realize the Great Harmony Society, (6) Implement the New Life Movement, (7) Confucius's spirit is immortal. The slogans for the commemorative meeting have also been determined by the city party headquarters as follows: (1) Confucius was a scholar who carried on the past and opened up the future, (2) Confucius was a great statesman who advocated civil rights, (3) Commemorating Confucius's birthday means emulating Confucius's personality, (4) Commemorating Confucius's birthday means carrying forward Confucius's doctrine, (5) Commemorating Confucius's birthday means restoring the nation's inherent culture, (6) Commemorating Confucius's birthday means promoting the nation's inherent spirit, (7) Commemorating Confucius's birthday means realizing the Great Harmony Society, (8) Commemorating Confucius's birthday means implementing the New Life Movement, (9) Commemorating Confucius's birthday means adhering to Confucius's teachings, (10) Confucius's spirit is immortal.

Below is Lian Zhenbo's original letter.

Saving a Disaster Victim is Saving a Life

Donate one more cent, save one more life

I recently read in your newspaper that a strong man in China is saving his daily tram fare to help the disaster victims, and I admire this very much. Now I am pre-paying one month of the one dime candy and vegetable expenses given to me by my parents every day, so that I have three yuan, which I send to your newspaper office and ask you to forward it to the disaster victims to do my best as an ordinary person. I also hope that all compatriots at home and abroad, as well as students of all sizes, will continue to follow suit and do their best to help each other, then the people will be very fortunate. (Below is written) Lian Zhenbo, a fifth-grade student from Guangdong Elementary School

Various Institutions Implement the Essentials of a "Three-Huas" Lifestyle; New Life Movement Association Announces Implementation Starting Last Month 81

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association believes that the implementation of the New Life Movement should start with various institutions. Therefore, it has formulated the "Preliminary Plan for Implementing the Militarization, Productization, and Artization of Life by Shanghai Institutions" based on the "Preliminary Implementation Plan for the Militarization, Productization, and Artization of Life" issued by the General Association. It adopts the principle of gradual progress and implements it in phases. The key points of the first phase have been prepared and printed into exquisite single sheets of "Haiyue Letter Paper." These were distributed yesterday to various national and municipal institutions in the city, one copy for each civil servant (if there are omissions or insufficiencies, please write to us). The original text of the Association's official letter and key points are recorded below:

Official Letter to Various Institutions

Previously, we received a notice from the New Life Movement Promotion Association, issuing the "Preliminary Implementation Plan for the Militarization, Productization, and Artization of Life," ordering us to formulate and gradually implement an implementation plan based on local conditions. We immediately formulated a preliminary plan for Shanghai institutions to implement a "Three-Huas" lifestyle, along with a set of key points for the first phase. These will be implemented first by civil servants in various institutions in the city, with the heads of each institution responsible for supervising and promoting the implementation. It is stipulated that each phase will last for two months, with this phase starting in September. We are sending you several copies of the key points, and we hope you will examine them and distribute them to your subordinates, one copy for each person, to be placed on their desks to facilitate implementation. We extend our official regards.

Key Points for the First Phase

Preliminary Plan for Implementing a "Three-Huas" Lifestyle in Shanghai Institutions, Key Points for the First Phase (implemented from September 1, 1935) (Principles) (1) To cultivate swift, orderly, and neat actions; (2) To cultivate a life of labor and thrift; (3) To cultivate habits of courtesy and law-abidingness. (A) Pertaining to Militarization: (1) Should be punctual (including office hours, meeting times, and social engagement times, etc.); (2) Clothing should be neat and simple (preferably wearing domestically produced uniforms); (3) All places should be kept clean and tidy. (B) Pertaining to Productization: (1) Implement savings or insurance for civil servants; (2) Do not excessively send out invitations for weddings and funerals; for other occasions such as birthdays, childbirth, and relocation, no invitations should be sent out except to relatives; (3) Gifts for celebrations and condolences should not exceed four yuan at most, and bank gift certificates or cash should be preferred. (C) Pertaining to Artization: (1) Treat people with a friendly attitude; (2) Manners should be dignified and polite; (3) The environment should be arranged in an aesthetically pleasing and practical manner. (Explanation) (1) These key points are based on the implementation plan issued by the General Association, taking into account the actual situation in Shanghai. They will be implemented in phases, starting from the basics and gradually progressing. (2) Civil servants of various institutions are role models for the citizens, so they must first implement the "Three-Huas" lifestyle. (3) The heads of each institution are fully responsible for supervising and promoting these key points. (4) Each phase of these key points will last for two months. During the implementation, the New Life Movement Association may send personnel to inspect at any time. Printed by the Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association.

Long-Distance Telephone Service Connecting Jiangsu and Zhejiang to Commence on September 1st; Time Limit Changed to Three Minutes Per Call 82

The Jiangsu Telecommunications Administration of the Ministry of Transportation, in conjunction with the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau, issued a notice stating that Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are prosperous areas for commerce in the country and also the political center. The need for long-distance telephone services is extremely urgent. Therefore, in recent years, cities and larger towns in the two provinces have gradually installed and connected to the network. For the sake of further development, both parties have agreed on measures for mutual long-distance telephone communication between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to handle communication matters between the two provinces. Starting from September 1st, all locations along the Beijing-Shanghai line in Jiangsu Province can be connected to various locations in Zhejiang Province via Yixing, Shanghai, Songjiang, Pingwang, and other bureaus. Those in Zhejiang Province who wish to call Jiangsu Province can do the same. According to international regulations, the call time will be changed from five minutes to three minutes per call. The pricing standard will be changed from pole line distance to spatial distance. In the future, after implementation, not only will communication be faster and prices lower, but the relationship between the two provinces will definitely be closer. It is truly a case of "a thousand miles apart, breathing can communicate." The convenience for people from all walks of life to communicate is truly not insignificant. In addition to a separate price list for reference, fearing that it may not be widely known, this notice is hereby issued.

At the same time, the Jiangsu Telecommunications Administration of the Ministry of Transportation also issued Notice No. 1393, stating that it had received Instruction No. 3778 from the Ministry of Transportation's Telecommunications Department, which stated that long-distance telephone calls in European and American countries are all based on a three-minute system. In order to meet international telephone standards and connect to international long-distance calls in the future, the Ministry has decided to change the long-distance call time in this area and Jiangsu and Zhejiang from five minutes to three minutes according to international regulations. The telephone rate will be based on spatial distance, effective from September 1st. (The following is omitted) We are instructed to comply and report accordingly. This notice is hereby issued, announcing that starting from September 1st, the call time for long-distance calls in this area and Jiangsu and Zhejiang will be changed from five minutes to three minutes, and a revised telephone rate list will be reissued for reference. In addition to sending separate letters, fearing that it may not be widely known, this notice is hereby issued.

Residents of Jin Shenfu Road and Lafeide Road in the French Concession of this city are opposed to the French Municipal Council increasing house tax by two to five times in July of this year. The original letter and tax increase table are excerpted below:

Request for Negotiation

Respected Sirs, on the 7th of this month, the French Municipal Council sent people to our residences to collect house tax for July of this year, suddenly increasing the amount by two or three times the previous amount, or even four or five times. We believe that our residences are mostly old and dilapidated. At this time of economic downturn and lack of prosperity in various industries, with increasing unemployment, it is difficult to maintain the old taxes, how can we bear such heavy taxes? Moreover, because of the reduction in rents in various places, house taxes have also fallen accordingly. Not only have we not enjoyed the benefits of tax reductions, but we have suffered the misfortune of this harsh tax. Therefore, we have specially jointly written to your association, requesting you to uphold justice and negotiate with the French Municipal Council in a practical manner. We are extremely hopeful. Addressed to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association in the French Concession.

The Rent Reduction Associations in various districts held a joint meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Huaguang Elementary School in Nanlinli, Xinjiang Road. These will include Cai Qiajun and Ye Qichang from the Zhabei District; Liu Xiaotian, He Yuqing, and Zhu Xiaqing from the Hongkou District; Zhang Binghua, Che Shouchun, and Hu Jia from the Pudong District; Wang Maoqing, Shan Xingwu, and Li Chuangen from the Xinzha District; Huang Xianggu, Qu Zhenhua, and Ye Ruizhai from the Second Special District; Zheng Jianbo, Du Chunsun, and Qiu Yaoshan from the Hudong District; Zhu Wenbo, Qin Linsheng, and Wu Yuwen from the Huxi District; and Ni Yiguan, Shen Xinfu, and Ling from the Hunan District. The executive committee members will convene a meeting to produce the supervisory committee. (2) Discuss the city-wide rent reduction plan. Please make a public decision on the case to be handled by the executive committee. (3) Petition the Sixth Plenary Session to stipulate rent reduction regulations. Please make a public decision on the case. (Resolution) Each district association will collect seals from residents and then elect representatives (one from each district) to go to Beijing to petition. Representatives from the entire city will also be sent to the station to see off the representatives going to Beijing (travel expenses self-funded). (4) Convene a general meeting of representatives from branch associations in various districts. Please make a public decision on the case. (Resolution) It is scheduled for 2:00 PM on September 16th, with the location to be arranged by the executive committee. Each district association should notify its branch associations to attend the meeting on time. (5) The date of the executive committee's inauguration and the location of the association are to be publicly decided on. (Resolution) It is scheduled for 2:00 PM on the 28th of this month, with the location temporarily set at Huaguang Elementary School. (6) Should the association issue a declaration? (A letter to landlords throughout the city and a letter to tenants). The case was approved.

Appealing for Rent Reduction The Joint Association sent a letter to landlords throughout the city appealing for rent reduction, stating: To all landlords in the city, may you be aware that the severity of the current era is unparalleled, and the magnitude of the situation is different from the past. This is known to all people in the country. Tracing back to the great world economic panic that occurred in the 18th year of the Republic of China, and continuing to this day, rural areas went bankrupt first, followed by urban collapse. Factories closed down, businesses ceased operations, and the number of unemployed citizens reached more than 500,000. The depletion of finance and the depression of the market are beyond description. How can we survive in this serious crisis? Moreover, the invading forces of the great powers are advancing rapidly and irresistibly. For us, the past of "treading on frost and firm ice" has already passed, and the present of "stripping the bed and reaching the skin" is coming. Unemployment is increasing day by day, and society is becoming increasingly unstable. At this time, the only way is to rise up urgently to save ourselves, seek common solutions, use clear understanding to understand subtle changes, use the talent and wisdom of the masses, turn the tide, and promote the practice of rent reduction, calling for reduced rents everywhere, seeking to achieve the goal. We respectfully ask all landlords in the city to understand our sincerity, agree to voluntarily reduce rents, do your best to do what is in line with humanity, alleviate the people's difficulties, and revive people's livelihoods.

A Letter to Tenants The association also sent a letter to tenants, stating: Comrades and compatriots throughout the city, in the state of world depression, our economy is in a state of decline. Recalling the two incidents of January 28th and January 28th, our people's attempts to gradually recover and the past dream of prosperity have been shattered. At this critical moment of survival, we should unite to save our own future. The paper image of singing and dancing in a time of peace has been torn apart by the power of the times. Today, the people of Shanghai are unemployed and committing suicide, all suffering from the economic collapse and the reasons for the market depression. Therefore, comparing Shanghai five years ago with the Shanghai of today is a great setback. Since our road to life is in a situation of irreparable disaster, please think about it, compatriots. Since the environment we are in is so bad, isn't the rent you pay still the same as before? We must reduce our own burden and start with self-help first. Feeling the crisis of the Chinese people, and with weak personal abilities, therefore, the most effective method of self-help that we can implement is to organize a rent reduction committee to reduce our burden, plan for the revival of people's livelihoods, and use the power of the masses to support our small contributions and strive together in the national economy. Compatriots, please be sure to rise up and work hard to reduce your own burden.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Explains That There Is No Maximum Limit to the Progressive Stamp Tax on Insurance Policies, etc. 89

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter yesterday to the Zhonghua Book Company, instructing on the stamp tax method for insurance policies, mortgages, etc.: (1) The stamp tax rate for insurance policies in Article 14 of the tax rate table is based on a stamp tax unit of every 1,000 yuan. 2 cents of stamp tax for 1,000 yuan, 4 cents of stamp tax for 2,000 yuan, and so on. However, if the total amount of the policy is more than 1,000 yuan but less than 2,000 yuan, the excess amount, even if it is less than one unit, is calculated as one unit. For example, if the insured amount is 1,500 yuan, the stamp tax should be affixed according to the 2,000 yuan example. (2) The loan or mortgage documents in Article 19 of the tax rate table are progressively stamped and have no maximum limit. Each 100 yuan is a unit, and the unit increases, and the tax rate also increases by 2 cents. For example, 2 yuan for 10,000 yuan, and 200 yuan for 1 million yuan. This is the biggest key difference between the new tax law and the old regulations.

Citizen Qin Yanwa and Others in Shanghai County are Organizing the Shanghai County Local Association 92

Citizen Qin Yanwa and others in Shanghai County, in order to promote local affairs, initiated the organization of the Shanghai County Local Association. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the initiators' meeting was held at the Daquanfu Restaurant in Old Four Doors. Those present included Yao Huiquan, Shi Ansheng, Qiao Nianchun, Zhang Jingye, Zhang Yi, Peng Yinqiao, Wang Chengyao, Xing Zhigang, Shi Yangyong, Qin Yanwa, Kang Jichang, and more than 30 others. Qin Yanwa chaired the meeting, reporting on the significance of initiating the organization of the association, and then formulating brief articles of association and deciding to temporarily use No. 209 Duojia Road, Fushi as the preparatory office. The brief articles of association are recorded as follows: Article 1: The purpose of this association is to strive for the welfare of the people, connect the feelings of all sectors, and assist the progress of local undertakings. Article 2: The members of this association are divided into the following three types: (1) The initiators of this association; (2) Representatives of various public organizations; (3) Volunteers to join this association, who must be introduced by two or more members and approved by the board of directors. Anyone who supports the purpose of this association or makes economic or technical contributions may be hired as an honorary member of this association upon the proposal of the board of directors and approved by the general meeting. Article 3: This association shall establish a board of directors, which shall elect one chairman, two vice-chairmen, and twelve directors from among the members, all of whom shall be unpaid and serve a term of two years, and may be re-elected. This association shall have one secretary, who shall handle the internal affairs of the association under the direction of the chairman and vice-chairmen, and shall be appointed by the board of directors. Article 5: This association shall hold a general meeting once every quarter and a board of directors meeting once a month. When necessary, temporary meetings may be held, all of which shall be convened by the chairman. Article 6: Members of this association shall pay an annual membership fee of two yuan, paid in one lump sum. When necessary, after a resolution by the general meeting, members shall contribute according to their ability. Article 7: The address of this association is No. 209 Duojia Road, Nanshi. Article 8: The detailed rules of this association will be formulated separately. Article 9: These articles of association shall be approved by the general meeting of members and submitted to the Party and government authorities for record.

Bureau of Social Affairs Bans Illegal Fees by Boiled Water Guild 94

Recently, the Boiled Water Shop Trade Association of this city has been arbitrarily collecting water fees and membership certificate fees from its members, violating regulations. The members reported this to the Bureau of Social Affairs for investigation and prohibition. After investigation, the Bureau of Social Affairs confirmed the facts and, in addition to sending a letter to the Public Security Bureau ordering its subordinates to ban it, also issued a public notice strictly prohibiting it. The public notice stated in brief: "It is reported that the Shanghai Boiled Water Shop Trade Association has been dispatching people to collect membership certificate fees and water ladle fees without obtaining approval from this Bureau. This Bureau has dispatched personnel to investigate and confirmed the facts. In addition to sending a letter to the Public Security Bureau ordering its subordinates to ban it, this is urgently announced to all boiled water businesses in this city. If anyone dares to harass or extort these shops in the future, they should be immediately handed over to the nearest police officer for further investigation. This is the notice."

(4) Regarding the date for the second joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees, "Resolution": It is tentatively scheduled for early October, and a date will be set after soliciting opinions from out-of-town committee members. (5) Committee member Pang suggests drafting a work outline for the association and submitting it to the 4th Congress for discussion. "Resolution": Approved in principle, Jiang Zhenxun will draft it and submit it to the second joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees for discussion.

New News from Hongqiao Sanatorium: Wang Yihui Appointed Vice President 96

The Hongqiao Sanatorium in this city was built by Mr. Ding Fubao. Although its scale is not very large, its architecture and equipment are state-of-the-art. Moreover, it is located in western Shanghai, with a quiet environment, making it ideal for patients to recuperate. Since Mr. Yan Fuqing has been the director of the sanatorium, he has strived to develop both medical and administrative affairs, gradually becoming known to the public. The number of people seeking medical treatment has also been increasing day by day, especially in obstetrics and gynecology, which has become quite crowded. Therefore, Mr. Wang Yihui, director of obstetrics and gynecology at the National Shanghai Medical College, has been invited to be the vice president of the sanatorium to meet the needs of local people. Recently, the sanatorium, in view of the urgent need for medicine in the local area, has reduced the cost of first-class wards and changed the first-class wards from two to four yuan, in order to provide universal service. All other medical expenses have been stipulated separately so that local people can seek medical treatment according to their personal economic strength.

Xu Xueyu, Director of Shanghai Telephone Bureau, Completes Telephone Project in Sichuan; The Ba-Cheng-E Long-Distance Telephone is Completed and Open for Service 97

Xu Xueyu, Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, was specially appointed by the Ministry of Transportation to reorganize the long-distance telephone and telegraph lines between Ba County, Chengdu, and Emei in Sichuan Province, and various telephone projects in Chengdu City. Director Xu led his staff to Sichuan in early July, and large quantities of materials were successively transported to various sections. After active progress, the project was completed on the 24th of this month, and the voice quality is clear. The details are as follows: From Ba County through Yongchuan, Rongchang, Longchang, Neijiang, Zizhong, Ziyang, Jianyang, to Chengdu, is the Ba-Cheng line, which is 1,050 li long. From Chengdu through Xinjin, Meishan, Jiajiang, to Emei, is the Cheng-E line, which is more than 500 li long. Both lines are equipped with telegraph and telephone lines. The two lines pass through many high mountains and ridges, and the construction was quite difficult. Moreover, due to inconvenient transportation, the transportation of materials was extremely difficult. At the time, it was summer, with alternating rain and sunshine, and unstable cold and heat, and workers often suffered from diseases. The completion of more than 1,500 li of long-distance lines in such a short period of time is truly an unprecedented achievement in the country. It is said that the Chengdu city telephone system will also be completed and opened for service within the month.

Drowning at Riva-Luzern Village 98

The garden in Riva-Luzern Village, north of Suzhou Creek, has all kinds of recreational facilities, including a small river with several small boats for people to enjoy themselves. It costs one yuan per hour, or six jiao for half an hour. Swimming is also allowed, and young people flock to it. However, last spring, five male and female tourists were riding in two small boats, enjoying themselves on the river. Unexpectedly, joy turned to sorrow. The two small boats raced ahead side by side and suddenly collided, causing both small boats to capsize. Two men and women drowned on the spot. The local court was immediately requested to send personnel to verify the bodies and coffin. Afterwards, Wei Jiechen, the patrol officer of the Zhoujiaqiao police station under the Zengjiadu police station in charge, posted a notice to ban it to prevent the occurrence of danger after seeing the tragic situation. Unexpectedly, not long after, another tragedy occurred. At about 4 p.m. the day before yesterday, Shen Genyou (aged 19, from Ningbo, an apprentice at the Jushulu Science Printing and Iron Factory) was also learning to swim in the small river in the village. For some reason, he struggled after entering the water for a short time and sank to the bottom of the river without resurfacing. Another tourist noticed and called for help. Then, they tried to retrieve Shen Genyou, who was already gasping for breath and about to die. He was then taken to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road for treatment. However, Shen Genyou had been underwater for too long, and his internal organs were damaged and could not be saved. He soon died. Tracing the cause of the disaster, the organizers of the village were undeniably responsible for the inadequate facilities. Yesterday morning, Chen Yiqing, the local baojia of the 28th bao 4th tu, was ordered by the police to report to the local court for an autopsy. After receiving the report, the court dispatched Prosecutor Du Jiasheng and Examiner Shen Qixiu to the scene in the afternoon to verify that it was indeed a drowning. He was ordered to be coffined and prepared for further instructions.

At around 4:38 p.m. yesterday, a fire broke out at the Xinyu Gasoline Lamp Shop at 499 Guangdong Road. Immediately, black smoke billowed and flames soared, making it impossible to control. The fire scene was then extinguished by the Central Fire Brigade. It is estimated that one floor was burned down, and the loss was very large. Fire insurance was held.

Huang Xianyao's Forgery Case Concluded; Sentencing on the 31st 101

Huang Xianyao, the second son of the late Huang Chuqiu, the founder of the Gongfa Company, the Riyue Bank, and the Great World Amusement Park from Shaoxing Yuyao, is 31 years old this year and works at the Zhongxi Drugstore on the Fourth Road. Previously, in order to defraud his father-in-law, Zhou Songqing, a local, of money, he colluded with lawyer Mi Jingshen (now withdrawn from the association) and Mi's clerk, Wu Jiajin, to forge a document from Zhou Songqing stating that he would preserve Huang's property. When the major event was over, 100,000 yuan would be distributed to Xianyao's family and handed over to him for safekeeping. First, he filed a petition for mediation against Zhou in the Shanghai District Court, but it failed. The document was placed in a safe deposit box at the Guohua Bank. Later, Wang Shaozeng, a creditor of Gongfa Company, found a photograph of the document and hired lawyer Xu Yannian to file a private prosecution in the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court against Zhou Songqing and Huang Xianyao, a son-in-law, for damaging creditors' rights. After repeated summons, Huang consistently refused to appear in court, and only Zhou appeared in court, denying that he had issued the document or that he had been entrusted with managing property. Later, the court ordered the issuance of an arrest warrant to arrest Huang. After Huang was arrested, personnel were sent to the Guohua Bank to open the safe deposit box and obtain the original document. Zhou Songqing then filed a lawsuit with the French Concession police against Huang Xianyao for forging the document, causing the creditor's rights damage case to be suspended, pending the investigation and public prosecution by the French Concession police, and the French Concession police took Huang Xianyao for investigation (the Criminal Court ordered a deposit of 50,000 yuan from a shop guarantor, but without a guarantor, he was detained in the detention center). As a result, enlarged photographs of the document were taken and identified by experts, confirming that it was not written by Zhou Songqing. Huang was then sent to the Second Special District Court, and the police department filed a public prosecution for forgery. After repeated hearings by Judge Li Changnian, Huang confessed that the co-defendants Mi Jingshen and Wu Jiajin had left Shanghai and could not be arrested. He was ordered to reschedule the hearing and await the suspension of the investigation of the previous case file. The situation has been reported in the previous two reports. However, the two defendants, Mi and Wu, have not yet been arrested. Yesterday morning, Judge Li of the Second Special District Court came to Criminal Court No. 1 and ordered Huang Xianyao to be brought for questioning. Huang's testimony was the same as that recorded in the previous report and will not be recorded again. The court then ordered the commencement of arguments. After the police department's lawyer, Gu Shouxi, and Huang's defense lawyer argued with each other, the court announced the conclusion and scheduled sentencing for the 31st of this month. Huang was still returned to the detention center.

Shanghai Magazine Company Publishes "Rare Treasures of Chinese Literature Series" 102

Ancient Chinese literature is as vast as the sea. In addition to classics, history, philosophy, and collections of writings, there are rare and valuable works that are not widely circulated. Moreover, poetry, prose, and novels published in the Ming Dynasty were often subject to Qing Dynasty bans, making them even more difficult to obtain. One volume, one edition, can easily cost hundreds of taels of silver, making them the exclusive domain of collectors. The Shanghai Magazine Company wants to realize the plan of making the series easier to record and popularizing the treasures. It has requested Lu Jiye, A Ying, Shi Zhecun, and others to search for rare books and borrow handwritten copies, selecting 50 types to compile the first series of "Rare Treasures of Chinese Literature." Based on the first edition of the best edition, sentences are carefully punctuated and proofread, totaling 10 million words, printed into more than 20,000 pages, and divided into 70 thick volumes. Starting from mid-September, one type will be published every Saturday, ranging from 200,000 to 600,000 words, antique and precious, packed in a wooden box, neat and beautiful. To suit the reader's time and economy, pre-orders will be sold for one month starting today. The entire series costs only fifteen yuan, plus one yuan and five jiao for shipping outside the city. The book box costs three yuan. The name of the purchaser can be engraved. The pre-order price is cheap. The first edition will not be sufficient to cover costs unless it reaches 2,000 copies. The pre-order catalog and samples are printed separately and can be requested. The publications for September include Yuan Xiaoxiu's Diary, Liuting's Poetry Talk, Jin Ping Mei, Initial Slaps on the Table, Lyrics of Sixty Famous Song Dynasty Poets, Collection of Tang Dynasty Legends, Complete Collection of Song Dynasty Zaju, and A Brief Record of Sights and Objects in the Imperial Capital, all of which are famous and valuable.

Prosecutor Xiao Jinying's Home Robbed 103

Xiao Jinying, a prosecutor at the Shanghai District Court, resides at No. 8, Hulin Lane, Jiandao Bridge, Humin South Extension Road, west of the court, which is a single shikumen building. What was stored in the suitcase in Xiao's house is unknown). Xiao immediately opened a list and reported to the Ximen Branch Bureau, requesting an investigation. It is said that the thieves dared to gather a crowd and rob the prosecutor's home in broad daylight with weapons, truly fearing no law.

Brave Detective Police of Ximen Capture Robbers; Gunfire Flies; Robbery of a Pawnshop Owner's Wife in the French Concession; Male and Female Robbers Use Pepper Powder; One Robber Shot, One Policeman Injured; Many Passersby Injured; Suspects Apprehended 104

At around 11:00 a.m. yesterday, a robbery of a pawnshop owner's wife by three robbers (two men and one woman) occurred at the intersection of Route Lafayette and Route du Marche in the French Concession. The amount robbed was 1,200 yuan. The robbers fled into the Chinese Concession after obtaining the loot, crossing the French Concession iron fence. The entire detective team of the Ximen Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and the heads of various police stations, bravely surrounded and captured them. The robbers fired guns along the way to resist arrest. The two sides exchanged fire more than a hundred times. As a result, one robber was shot and captured, one policeman was injured, and stray bullets injured many passersby. Four suspects were intercepted. At that time, the order in the Tangjiawan area was very chaotic, and it took about three quarters of an hour to restore order. The details are as follows:

Woman Sends Money

Zhu Qiuhui, 39 years old, from Huizhou, is a shareholder of the Qiaoyuan Pawnshop at No. 31 Chengyuli, Route du Marche, French Concession. Zhu works at the pawnshop. The pawnshop has long been in contact with the Guangda Pawnshop on nearby Rue Baille. Therefore, when both pawnshops are short of money, they often accommodate each other, which is customary. Because Shanghai is unstable, in order to avoid attracting the attention of robbers, Qiaoyuan sends Zhu's wife, Wu (37 years old, from the same hometown as Zhu), to take money whenever money is needed.

Using Pepper Powder to Blind

At about 11:20 a.m. yesterday, Zhu sent his wife to Guangda to take money. Wu walked alone to Guangda, obtained 1,200 silver dollars, and hid the money in her pocket. As she turned to return along the original road, three robbers, two men and one woman, suddenly jumped out from the roadside. The two men were wearing short clothes, each holding a pistol, and forbade Wu to make any noise. One of the robbers even used pepper powder that had been prepared in advance, and threw it into Wu's eyes. Wu was caught off guard and was blinded.

Shouting "Catch the Robbers"

At the same time, one robber went forward and robbed all 1,200 silver dollars from Wu. The three robbers obtained the loot, entered Nanshengli from Route du Marche North, crossed the French Concession iron fence to the Tangjiawan small vegetable market, and fled along Xilin Houlou. Although Wu's eyes were blinded by the pepper powder, she still chased desperately. Shouting "Catch the robbers," the police whistle sounded on the road. The robbers knew that things were bad and ran along Fangxie Road through Xilin Houlou, firing guns along the way. At that time, Police Officer Li Rongsheng of Post No. 12 and Police Officer Li Zhenbai of Post No. 15 of the Ximen Branch of the Public Security Bureau heard the alarm and rushed to the scene. They met the robbers head-on, and the two sides exchanged fire. During the exchange of fire, Police Officer Li Zhenbai was hit by a bullet in the foot and immediately fell to the ground. However, Police Officer Li Rongsheng still pursued closely. When he chased to the intersection of Fangxie Branch Road, Shen Wenda, the squad leader of the detective team of the Ximen Branch, had heard the alarm and, together with Deputy Squad Leader Luo Weixin, Team Leader Li Taochen, Yu Ruhai, Chen Enrong, Jiao Baojun, Zheng Yongxiang, Yang Jisheng, Bian Wenguang, and other detectives, advanced from Wansheng Road southward and from Fangxie Road. They met the robbers in front of the Kongtongsheng Clock and Watch Shop, and the two sides began fighting again. The sound of gunfire was like a string of pearls, totaling seventy or eighty shots.

Original Stolen Money Recovered

At this time, the robbers had fallen into encirclement. With many detectives in front and pursuing police in the rear, they fought desperately, hoping to escape. However, because the gunshots were too fierce, one robber was shot and fell in front of Brothers Shop Nos. 146-147 Fangxie Road, and was captured. A pistol No. 886 was seized, and 110 yuan of the original stolen money was recovered. At the same time, Branch Chief Police Officer Li also supervised a large number of police officers to pursue and intercept at various key roads. As a result, four more suspects were apprehended, brought to the bureau, and interrogated one by one.

Many Robbers Intercepted

The robber who was intercepted on the spot, Hong Chen Hongyuan, 44 years old, from Qingjiang, admitted that he had colluded with the gang to commit robbery. The other four suspects were: Zhao Baoyou, 27 years old, from Anhui; Fan Fangtai, 26 years old, from Jiangxi; Lin Shungen, 19 years old, from Wuxi; and Shi Yunzhang, 48 years old, from Yangzhou. The injured Police Officer Li Zhenbai and the injured robber Chen Hongyuan were sent to the hospital for treatment first. The rest were detained for investigation. However, because the robber Chen Hongyuan had a minor injury to his foot, he was bandaged and immediately led the team for interrogation.

Stray Bullets Injure Passersby

During the fierce battle, bullets flew everywhere and injured many passersby. They include: Lu Honggen, 42 years old, from Dongtai, a laborer, slightly injured; Zhao Tingdong, 43 years old, from Funing, a rickshaw puller, severely injured in the arm bone; Lu Fulai, 26 years old, from Fujian, an assistant at No. 147 Zhaozhou Road, shot in the chest, which is very dangerous; Sun Jinji, 44 years old, from Shaoxing, injured in the arm; and Du Yang, a woman, 28 years old, from Wujiang, who was sitting in an employment agency on Xilin Road at the time, injured in the legs and arms. The above persons were all taken to the Shanghai Hospital by Branch Chief Police Officer Li for treatment. In addition, a car with license No. 4837 of the Xiang Sheng Automobile Company was also hit by stray bullets, with a hole pierced in the right door. In addition to immediately reporting to Director Cai, Branch Chief Police Officer Li also ordered his subordinates to strictly arrest the remaining accomplices.

Yu Changzi's Case of Breach of Trust and False Prosecution; Plaintiff Requests Change of Jurisdiction; Whether the Trial Should Be Handled by Other Courts is Up to the Superior Court to Decide; Both Lu Xihou and Yu Changzi Did Not Appear in Court Yesterday 105

Yu Changzi, a judge of the Civil Court of the Shanghai First Special District Court, was handling the case of Lu Xihou, chairman of the board of directors of the China Industrial Bank, applying for the bank to be declared bankrupt and sending personnel to clear its accounts after the bank went bankrupt. Many people originally planned to go to the court to listen to the proceedings. It happened that at 1:00 p.m., the sky suddenly became overcast, followed by thunderstorms. He also did not appear in court yesterday. His lawyer appeared in court and said that Lu was not in Shanghai. Judge Wu, because both parties had not appeared in court, and the plaintiff had petitioned for a change of jurisdiction, immediately instructed that "the case has been petitioned by the plaintiff for a change of jurisdiction, and the matter will be handled according to law after the higher court has ruled," and adjourned court.
